RUS_Economy_decisions = {
	RUS_complete_land_reform = {
		icon = GFX_decision_POL_looming_peasants_strike

		allowed = { always = no } #activated by effect
		available = { always = no }
		cancel_trigger = { 
			NOT = { has_idea = rus_unfinished_land_reform }
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 365

		fire_only_once = yes
		
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 2
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout RUS_complete_land_reform"
			set_country_flag = RUS_land_reform_failure
			if = {
				limit = { RUS_denikin_in_power = yes }
				hidden_effect = { country_event = rusd.3208 }
			}
			else = {
				add_stability = -0.15
				RUS_decrease_ruling_party_pop_large = yes
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = soviet_russia_restored }
					add_ideas = RUS_rural_unrest_soviet_russia
				}
				else = {
					add_ideas = RUS_rural_unrest_2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { 
						check_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^1 = 1 }
						plsr_in_power = yes
					}
				}
				RUS_increase_plsr_pop = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { 
						check_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^2 = 1 }
						nsp_in_power = yes
					}
				}
				RUS_increase_nsp_pop = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { 
						check_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^3 = 1 } 
						psr_in_power = yes
					}
				}
				RUS_increase_psr_pop = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { 
						check_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^4 = 1 }
						rsdrp_in_power = yes
					}
				}
				RUS_increase_rsdrp_pop = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { 
						check_variable = { Duma_Party_Status^14 = 1 }
						RUS_savinkov_pm = yes
						RUS_savinkov_in_power = yes
						has_country_flag = nrpr_banned 
					}
				}
				RUS_increase_nrpr_pop = yes
			}			
		}
	}
	RUS_Develop_Civilian_Industry_In_State = {
		name = RUS_Develop_Industry_In_State
		icon = generic_construction

		allowed = { always = no } #activated by effect

		available = {
			FROM = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 2
		}

		cost = 25
		days_remove = 60
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 2
		}
		state_target = yes

		
		modifier = { consumer_goods_factor = 0.04 }

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 2
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove RUS_Develop_Civilian_Industry_In_State"
			FROM = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
				increase_state_category_by_one_level = yes
			}
		}
	}

	RUS_chelyabinsk_tractor_plant = {

		days_remove = 120
		fire_only_once = yes
		modifier = { consumer_goods_factor = 0.04 }
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 2
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove RUS_chelyabinsk_tractor_plant"
			572 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
				add_building_construction = { type = industrial_complex level = 3 }
				add_victory_points = { province = 9292 value = 8 }
				add_resource = {
					type = steel
					amount = 24
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = unlock_chtz
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc_aat = no }
				custom_effect_tooltip = available_designer
				show_ideas_tooltip = chelyabinskiy_traktornyy
			}
			else = {
				unlock_military_industrial_organization_tooltip = mio:RUS_chelyabinskiy_traktornyy_organisation
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

	RUS_izhevsk_mechanical_plant = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_merge_plant_tank
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = {
			FROM = { is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT }
		}
		highlight_states = { highlight_state_targets = { state = 399 } } #Izhevsk
		cost = 75
		state_target = yes
		days_remove = 60
		fire_only_once = yes
		modifier = { consumer_goods_factor = 0.04 }
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 2
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision complete RUS_izhevsk_mechanical_plant"
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove RUS_izhevsk_mechanical_plant"
			399 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
				add_building_construction = { type = arms_factory level = 2 }
			}
			if = { #Tooltip for those that have MIOs
				limit = { has_dlc_aat = yes }
				mio:RUS_izjevskij_mekhanitsjeskij_organisation = {
					add_mio_size = 2
					add_mio_funds = 1000
				}
			}
			else = { #Tooltip for those that have vanilla companies
				custom_effect_tooltip = {
					localization_key = RUS_unlock_improved_company COMPANY = izjevskij_mekhanitsjeskij
				}
				show_ideas_tooltip = izjevskij_mekhanitsjeskij_improved
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = izjevskij_mekhanitsjeskij }
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = izjevskij_mekhanitsjeskij
						add_idea = izjevskij_mekhanitsjeskij_improved
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = improve_imz
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
	}

				add = 2

		}

				target_province = 9292
			}
		}

RUS_Zemstvo_Funding_decisions = {
	RUS_Invest_In_The_Northern_Zemstva = {
		icon = generic_construction

		available = {
			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 1
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_funding_zemstva }
		}
		visible = {
			OR = {
				controls_state = 263 #Novgorod
				controls_state = 208 #Luga
				controls_state = 244 #Volkhov
				controls_state = 264 #Tikhvin

		}

	### Default decisions first ###
	RUS_Attack_Country_default = {
		name = RUS_Attack_Region
		icon = hol_draw_up_staff_plans
		allowed = { always = no }  #activated manually 
		available = {
			can_declare_war_on = FROM
			OR = {
				is_owner_neighbor_of = FROM
				any_allied_country = { is_owner_neighbor_of = FROM }
				any_subject_country = { is_owner_neighbor_of = FROM }
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { tag = AUS } }
					FROM = { any_allied_country = { is_owner_neighbor_of = ROOT } }
				} 
			}
			NOT = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = FROM }
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = AFG } }
				FROM = { 
					NOT = { has_country_flag = AFG_aral_success }
				}
			} 
			if = {
				limit = { 
					is_in_faction_with = GER 
					FROM = { tag = FIN }
				}
				FIN = { FIN_is_monarchy = no }
			}
		}
		visible = {
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { is_in_europe = yes } }
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = { is_ally_with = GER }
					}
					NOT = { has_global_flag = danzig_treaty_active }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = { is_ally_with = GER }
					}
					NOT = { has_global_flag = budapest_treaty_active }
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 10
		days_remove = 30
		fire_only_once = yes
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		war_with_target_on_remove = yes

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				RUS_dont_attack_if_vulnerable_or_preparing = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { RUS_dont_attack_if_target_is_stronger = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { RUS_dont_attack_if_faction_is_stronger = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { RUS_dont_attack_if_overlord_is_stronger = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { tag = PER }
				country_exists = GER
				NOT = { FROM = { has_war_with = TUR } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { tag = AFG }
				country_exists = GER
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { tag = POL }
				has_game_rule = { rule = POL_foreign_policy option = POL_FOREIGN_POLICY_RUSSIA }
			}
		}

		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision cancel RUS_Attack_Country_default target: [From.GetName]"
			clear_decision_attack_AI = yes
			add_political_power = 10
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision complete RUS_Attack_Country_default target: [From.GetName]"
			FROM = { incoming_war_notification_effect = yes }
			setup_decision_attack_AI = yes
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove RUS_Attack_Country_default target: [From.GetName]"
			clear_decision_attack_AI = yes
			declare_war_on = {
				target = FROM
				type = annex_everything
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = FIN } }
				activate_mission = RUS_defeat_finland
				FIN = { activate_mission = FIN_survive_russia }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = MON } }
				activate_mission = RUS_defeat_mongolia
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					FROM = { 
						OR = {
							tag = GEO 
							tag = AZE 
							tag = MTR 
							tag = DAG 
							tag = ARM 
						}
					}
				}
				activate_mission = RUS_defeat_caucasus
			}
		}
	}

				set_temp_variable = { china_infantry_equipment_ratio = FROM.num_equipment_in_armies@infantry_equipment }
				divide_temp_variable = { china_infantry_equipment_ratio = FROM.num_target_equipment_in_armies@infantry_equipment }

				set_temp_variable = { china_purchase_infantry_equipment_factor = 1 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { china_purchase_infantry_equipment_factor = china_infantry_equipment_ratio }
				multiply_temp_variable = { china_purchase_infantry_equipment_factor = 20 }

				add = china_purchase_infantry_equipment_factor
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_war = yes
					has_equipment = { infantry_equipment < 6000 }
				}
			}

				}
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = RUS_USNS_counter_cost
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			command_power > var:RUS_USNS_cp_cost
			NOT = { has_equipment = { infantry_equipment < 750 } }
		}
		days_remove = 30
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 300
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				FROM = { is_core_of = UKR }
			}
		}
		state_target = yes
		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision complete RUS_counter_insurgency"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_temp_CP_cost = RUS_USNS_cp_cost }
				multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_temp_CP_cost = -1 }

					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -750
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {

					limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_belarus_resistance } }
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_belarus_resistance }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_forest_brothers_resistance } }
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_forest_brothers_resistance }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_polish_resistance } }
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_polish_resistance }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_ukrainian_resistance } }
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_ukrainian_resistance }
				}
				set_state_flag = RUS_USNS_removed
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = { is_core_of = UKR }
						ROOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_manshtein_UKR_governor }
					}

				}
				else = {

				}
			}
		}

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_agreement
		priority = 100

			}			
		}

		}
	}
	
	TRM_lose_morale_during_war = {
		allowed = { always = no }
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = TRM_losing_morale_off
					NOT = { has_war_with = RUS }
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					country_exists = RUS
					NOT = { is_ally_with = RUS }
				}
				AND = {
					country_exists = RVA
					NOT = { is_ally_with = RVA }
				}
				AND = {
					country_exists = WRA
					NOT = { is_ally_with = WRA }
				}
				AND = {
					country_exists = RRF
					NOT = { is_ally_with = RRF }
				}
			}			
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = TRM_losing_morale_off
					NOT = { has_war_with = RUS }
				}
			}
		}
		selectable_mission = no
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		days_mission_timeout = 30
		ai_will_do = { factor = 100 }
		
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout TRM_lose_morale_during_war"
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_with_trait = TRM_liberator_of_siberia }
				set_temp_variable = { change_morale = -0.05 }
				RUS_change_siberian_war_morale = yes
			}
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = { change_morale = -0.1 }
				RUS_change_siberian_war_morale = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					check_variable = { global.siberian_war_chance < 0.01 } 
					has_war_with = RUS
					if = {
						limit = { JAP = { is_ai = no } }
						JAP = { NOT = { has_war_with = RUS } }
					}
				}
				country_event = tram.501
			}
			else = {
				activate_mission = TRM_lose_morale_during_war
			}
		}
	}

	RUS_constitutional_drafting_mission = {
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_support
		priority = 100

		allowed = { always = no } #manually activated

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			RUS_denikin_in_power = no
		}
		
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		
		is_good = no
		selectable_mission = no
		days_mission_timeout = 200
		
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout RUS_constitutional_drafting_mission"			
			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_constitutional_drafting_mission_tt
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_idea = RUS_empowered_president }
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_constitutional_drafting_mission_tt2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							set_temp_variable = { RUS_vvsr_public_confidence = party_popularity@ruling_party }
							if = {
								limit = { is_in_coalition_with_market_liberal = yes }
								add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_vvsr_public_confidence = party_popularity@market_liberal }
							}
							if = {
								limit = { is_in_coalition_with_social_conservative = yes }
								add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_vvsr_public_confidence = party_popularity@social_conservative }
							}
							if = {
								limit = { is_in_coalition_with_authoritarian_democrat = yes }
								add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_vvsr_public_confidence = party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat }
							}
							if = {
								limit = { is_in_coalition_with_national_populist = yes }
								add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_vvsr_public_confidence = party_popularity@national_populist }
							}
							OR = {
								check_variable = { RUS_vvsr_public_confidence = 0.25 }
								check_variable = { RUS_vvsr_public_confidence > 0.25 }
							}
							check_variable = { RUS_vvsr_rovs_unity > 0.25 }
						}
						AND = {
							is_ai = yes
							has_game_rule = { rule = RUS_aftermath_of_kornilov option = RUS_AFTERMATH_OF_KORNILOV_DENIKIN_PRESIDENT }
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { RUS_vvsr_public_confidence > 0.59 }
						check_variable = { RUS_rovs_wrangel < 15 }
						NOT = { has_idea = RUS_empowered_president }
					}
					country_event = rusd.3220 # republic
				}
				else = {
					country_event = rusd.3221 # presidential dictatorship
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = rusd.3222 # collapse of the council
			}

		}
	}
